# Higham Chapter 16 Source Coverage Ledger

## Source and Scope

- Edition: Higham, *Accuracy and Stability of Numerical Algorithms*, 2nd ed. (SIAM, 2002), verified from `pdfinfo` title metadata and source DOI path.
- Chapter: 16, "The Sylvester Equation".
- Printed pages read: 305-319.
- Source file: `References/1.9780898718027.ch16.pdf`.
- Mode: core.
- Parallel split: 3B.
- Planning documents consulted: `chapter_splitting/HIGHAM_PARALLEL_FORMALIZATION_BLUEPRINT.md`, the Split 3B section of `chapter_splitting/split_primary_contracts.md`, and the Chapter 16 rows of `chapter_splitting/chapter_index.md`.
- Selected-scope gate: FAIL. Several central square-Frobenius results, the rectangular vec/Kronecker formulation, the diagonal (16.3) coefficient/solution foundation including separated coefficient bijectivity, common-entry singularity, sigma-min bounds, Gram-eigenvalue lower-bound certificates, determinant/nonsingularity consequences, and the concrete-left-inverse/op-norm route to coefficient/operator lower bounds are proved, including general Sylvester concrete-left-inverse and finite-Gram-eigenvalue routes to `SepLowerBound` and exact `sylvesterSepInf`. Conditional exact Schur-coordinate transform plus supplied diagonal-factor and triangular-factor solve/vectorized-coefficient/determinant bridges are proved, the real quasi-Schur factor existence and exact transform solution-equivalence surfaces are recorded, and the real quasi-triangular route now has a supplied adjacent two-column exact block-system lemma, block-vector coefficient equivalence, supplied inverse/left-inverse certificates for the two active block columns, previous-column recurrence uniqueness wrappers, right-inverse/left-inverse solve uniqueness wrappers, inverse-consistency wrappers, determinant/surjectivity/bijectivity consequences, and an active-block unique-solve theorem. The named (16.3) determinant/eigenvalue-separation iff is now proved for the real vec/Kronecker coefficient via complexification, and both the arbitrary complex coefficient and the complexified real coefficient have shifted determinant spectrum/difference characterizations. The Frobenius/`vec` norm bridge, coefficient sigma-min wrappers, product-index Gram-eigenvalue bridges for Sylvester and Lyapunov operators, exact Sylvester and Lyapunov `sylvesterSepInf` condition routes from both left-inverse and Gram data, supplied spectral-diagonal Lyapunov operator/coefficient/Gram lower-bound and `sep(A,-A^T)` lower-bound/source-shaped condition routes, the concrete-left-inverse and Gram Lyapunov sigma-min, sep, exact-infimum, first-order condition, condition-certificate witness, first-order wrappers, entrywise-gap first-order wrappers, and perturbation routes, the Sylvester Psi Gram certificate witness, the Lyapunov structured eta feasible-set/infimum model, the two-sided Lyapunov eta/xi infimum bridge plus attained minimizer, and the (16.29) practical max-entry/computed-residual budget bridge including raw and packaged monotone budget wrappers, scalar cap wrappers, generic residual-error-model wrappers, arbitrary-coefficient floating-point residual wrappers from supplied inverse certificates, a separated-diagonal floating-point scalar wrapper plus componentwise, monotone, and monotone scalar caps, and supplied diagonal/Schur-diagonal/Schur-triangular exact-inverse subcases with raw-budget, scalar, monotone, and monotone-scalar caps are proved. The full core pass still has open selected rows for automatic/unsupplied real-Schur block determinant and separation certificates, Hessenberg-Schur surfaces, rounded Schur residual arithmetic, exact automatic condition-number formulas, and LAPACK-style estimator paths.
- Selected-scope clarification: the remaining block-solve wording means automatic/unsupplied real-Schur block determinant and separation certificates outside the internally generated real-Schur/no-common route, Hessenberg-Schur surfaces, rounded solve residual arithmetic, and estimator paths. Supplied determinant/product-shift frontier schedules, generated-frontier wrappers, and the recursive generated-step candidate now close the exact Schur-coordinate traversal solution, original-coordinate reconstruction, and original-coordinate `ExistsUnique` wrappers under no common complex spectrum; the exact vec/Kronecker route also produces source-facing generated-step witnesses without requiring the formula predicate as a caller premise.
- Latest selected-scope additions: certificate raw computed-residual budget endpoints now also have scalar, monotone, and monotone-scalar variants for concrete-left-inverse, finite-Gram, and sigma-min hypotheses; strict-block-map real quasi-Schur factors now instantiate the raw computed-residual practical bound for the original coordinates; exact vectorized Sylvester and Lyapunov coefficient solutions are identified with the nonsingular-inverse solution under determinant, sigma-min, finite-Gram, and concrete-left-inverse certificates; strict real-quasi-Schur block-label hypotheses turn the Schur factor into the supplied triangular case and yield original-coordinate uniqueness from shifted determinant certificates; Sylvester and Lyapunov vec coefficients expose both nonsingular-inverse left and right actions under determinant, sigma-min, finite-Gram, and concrete-left-inverse certificates; concrete-left-inverse, Gram, and sigma certificates instantiate non-floating raw computed-residual budget practical endpoints; real quasi-Schur factors feed directly into the repository's exact Schur-coordinate Sylvester solution equivalence; determinant-nonzero square Sylvester vec coefficients instantiate raw computed-residual budget, monotone, scalar, and monotone-scalar practical endpoints; determinant/sigma-min/finite-Gram/concrete-left-inverse certificates expose explicit nonsingular-inverse solve actions for Sylvester and Lyapunov vec coefficients; entrywise gap hypotheses produce determinant/nonsingularity certificates for diagonal and supplied Schur-diagonal Sylvester coefficients plus diagonal and supplied spectral-diagonal Lyapunov coefficients; square Sylvester determinant, Gram, sigma-min, and concrete-left-inverse finite-op-norm certificates instantiate scalar, monotone, and monotone-scalar floating-point practical residual endpoints with the nonsingular inverse; the non-floating computed-residual and explicit error-model practical endpoints also have determinant-nonzero square coefficient variants; generic determinant and concrete-left-inverse finite-op-norm certificates yield finite-matrix, Sylvester, and Lyapunov vectorized bijectivity and unique-solve wrappers; and nonsingular shifted triangular column coefficients expose inverse, injectivity, surjectivity, bijectivity, unique-solve, active column-step, and column-step equality wrappers for the triangular recurrence.

- Latest real-Schur source-numbered alias wave: the real quasi-Schur factor-existence surface and the exact original-to-Schur-coordinate Sylvester equivalence now expose `H16_eq16_4_*` aliases for (16.4) and (16.4)-(16.5). - Latest direct zero-coupling solve-wrapper wave: the shifted determinant/product-zero bridge now feeds active-block injectivity, surjectivity, bijectivity, trivial-kernel, unique-solve, nonsingular-inverse solution-identification, supplied two-column block-system construction, and previous-column uniqueness wrappers without carrying quasi-Schur block-map hypotheses. These are exact algebraic wrappers for the degenerate branch, not the genuine coupled real-Schur separation proof.
- Latest coupled block-action packaging wave: the genuinely coupled two-column route now has explicit block matrices for the left `A` action and the supplied `2 x 2` Schur-block action, plus a proved equivalence between the existing coupled `u,v` equations and equality of those two block actions on the concatenated vector. The product-shift no-eigenvector route can consume a no-nonzero-block-action certificate directly; later spectral-transport and traversal wrappers now consume the resulting determinant/no-common data in the supplied exact traversal path.
- Latest direct block-kernel separation bridge: the supplied adjacent two-column coefficient kernel is now proved equivalent to equality of the left `A` block action and the supplied `2 x 2` Schur-block action on the same concatenated vector. Consequently, a no-nonzero-block-action certificate directly gives determinant nonsingularity for the two-column coefficient. This removes the product-shift detour from the eventual spectral-separation route, but still leaves the common-complex-eigenvalue/intertwiner theorem open.
- Latest two-column intertwining bridge: the coupled active-column equations now also have the standard matrix form `A * U = U * J`, where `U` packages the two active columns and `J` is the supplied adjacent real `2 x 2` Schur block. This gives the next spectral proof a conventional intertwiner surface while still leaving the complex shared-eigenvalue transfer open.
- Latest complex intertwiner eigenvector bridge: a general finite complex-matrix theorem now proves that any intertwiner `A * X = X * B` maps a supplied `B` eigenvector to an `A` eigenvector with the same eigenvalue, with a companion existential eigenpair wrapper when the image is nonzero. This closes a reusable algebraic dependency for the future real-Schur block-separation proof; the still-open part is producing a suitable nonzero image from the genuine `2 x 2` block spectral hypotheses.
- Latest real-to-complex intertwining bridge: rectangular real matrices now have a reusable entrywise complexification map preserving multiplication and intertwining identities, and the two-column `A * U = U * J` bridge has a complexified wrapper ready for the finite complex intertwiner/eigenvector theorem.
- Latest intertwiner kernel-invariance bridge: a general real-matrix lemma now proves that `A * U = U * J` makes the kernel of `U` invariant under `J`, with a two-column Schur-block specialization. This is the algebraic setup for the remaining irreducibility/no-real-invariant-line argument in the genuine coupled block case.
- Latest no-real-eigenline kernel bridge: determinant algebra for two real `Fin 2` columns now proves that a nonzero real intertwiner `A * U = U * J` has trivial kernel whenever the right-hand `2 x 2` block has no real eigenvector, with a two-column Schur-block specialization. This closes the irreducible-real-kernel dependency and leaves the complexified nonzero-image transfer as the next proof-risk step toward the no-block-action certificate.
- Latest complex nonzero-image bridge: a trivial real-kernel theorem now lifts through entrywise complexification, proving nonzero complex vectors remain nonzero under the complexified column-pair map in the no-real-eigenvector `2 x 2` block setting. - Latest determinant-to-matrix exact solve bridge: `existsUnique_isSylvesterSolutionRect_of_sylvesterVecCoeff_det_ne_zero` now turns any rectangular Sylvester vec/Kronecker determinant certificate into uniqueness and existence for the matrix equation `AX - XB = C`, and `H16_eq16_3_existsUnique_isSylvesterSolutionRect_of_sylvesterVecCoeff_det_ne_zero` exposes the same bridge as a source-numbered endpoint. - Latest exact Schur residual transport: `sylvesterResidualRect_schur_transform_identity` proves that, under supplied orthogonal Schur-coordinate factors and `Xhat = U Y V^T`, the original residual is exactly `U` times the Schur-coordinate residual times `V^T`; `H16_eq16_5_9_sylvesterResidualRect_schur_transform_identity` exposes that identity under the source-numbered transport convention. `frobNormRect_sylvesterResidualRect_schur_transform` then uses Frobenius invariance under orthogonal left/right multiplication to prove equality of the original and Schur-coordinate residual norms, with `H16_eq16_9_frobNormRect_sylvesterResidualRect_schur_transform` as its source-numbered alias. The wrapper `frobNormRect_sylvesterResidualRect_le_of_schur_transform` and alias `H16_eq16_9_frobNormRect_sylvesterResidualRect_le_of_schur_transform` transfer any supplied Schur-coordinate residual bound to the reconstructed original-coordinate iterate. The budget bridge `sylvesterComputedResidualBudget_of_schur_frobenius_error_model` / `H16_eq16_29_sylvesterComputedResidualBudget_of_schur_frobenius_error_model` turns a Schur-coordinate Frobenius residual-error model into the original-coordinate computed-residual budget with the same uniform radius. The conservative practical wrapper `sylvester_practical_error_bound_of_schur_transform_residual_bound` and `H16_eq16_29_sylvester_practical_error_bound_of_schur_transform_residual_bound` use `Rhat = 0` to feed a Schur-coordinate residual bound directly into the existing max-entry practical bound; `sylvester_practical_error_bound_of_schur_transform_residual_bound_scalar`, `sylvester_practical_error_bound_of_schur_transform_residual_bound_mono`, and `sylvester_practical_error_bound_of_schur_transform_residual_bound_mono_scalar` add the relative scalar-cap and estimator-facing monotone forms. The direct wrapper `sylvester_practical_error_bound_of_schur_frobenius_error_model` feeds a Schur-coordinate Frobenius residual-error certificate into the relative practical bound. The denominator-free companions `sylvester_practical_abs_error_bound_of_schur_transform_residual_bound` / `H16_eq16_29_sylvester_practical_abs_error_bound_of_schur_transform_residual_bound` and `sylvester_practical_abs_error_bound_of_schur_transform_residual_bound_scalar` / `H16_eq16_29_sylvester_practical_abs_error_bound_of_schur_transform_residual_bound_scalar` give unnormalized max-entry bounds. This closes the exact coordinate/norm/bound/budget transport layer used by (16.9) and (16.29), but not the rounded Schur/Bartels-Stewart residual arithmetic or QR/computed-path stability assumptions.
- Latest supplied Schur-triangular exact-solve aliases: `H16_eq16_4_6_existsUnique_isSylvesterSolutionRect_schurTriangular` now names the supplied upper-triangular Bartels-Stewart exact unique-solve theorem under equations (16.4)-(16.6); `H16_eq16_2_6_existsUnique_sylvesterVecCoeff_schurTriangular_mulVec` and `H16_eq16_3_sylvesterVecCoeff_schurTriangular_det_ne_zero` expose the corresponding vectorized unique-solve and determinant-nonsingularity surfaces. These are source-map aliases over existing exact theorems, not new rounded solver or residual-stability results.
- Latest generalized-equation residual surfaces: `H16_eq16_30_generalizedSylvesterAXB_CXD_residual_zero_iff_solution` gives the Chapter 16.5 equation (16.30) zero-residual characterization a source-numbered handle; `generalizedSylvesterPairResidualLeft`, `generalizedSylvesterPairResidualRight`, and `H16_eq16_31_generalizedSylvesterPair_residual_zero_iff_solution` add the same residual/equivalence surface for the coupled generalized Sylvester equations (16.31); and `H16_eq16_32_riccatiResidual_zero_iff_solution` does the same for the Riccati residual form (16.32). These are residual/equation equivalence surfaces, not new generalized-equation solvers.
- Latest no-common-eigenvalue practical residual wrappers: `sylvester_practical_error_bound_of_no_common_complex_right_eigenvalue_computed_residual_certificate` and its scalar/absolute/raw-budget/error-model variants now feed `NoCommonComplexRightEigenvalue (realMatrixToComplex A) (realMatrixToComplex B)` into the (16.29) practical max-entry residual bounds. These are source-facing wrappers over the closed determinant/nonsingular-inverse route, not rounded Schur-solve or estimator theorems.
- Latest no-common Schur-residual bridge: `sylvester_practical_error_bound_of_no_common_complex_right_eigenvalue_schur_transform_residual_bound`, `sylvester_practical_error_bound_of_no_common_complex_right_eigenvalue_schur_transform_residual_bound_scalar`, `sylvester_practical_error_bound_of_no_common_complex_right_eigenvalue_schur_transform_residual_bound_mono`, `sylvester_practical_error_bound_of_no_common_complex_right_eigenvalue_schur_transform_residual_bound_mono_scalar`, `sylvester_practical_abs_error_bound_of_no_common_complex_right_eigenvalue_schur_transform_residual_bound`, `sylvester_practical_abs_error_bound_of_no_common_complex_right_eigenvalue_schur_transform_residual_bound_scalar`, `sylvester_practical_abs_error_bound_of_no_common_complex_right_eigenvalue_schur_transform_residual_bound_mono`, and `sylvester_practical_abs_error_bound_of_no_common_complex_right_eigenvalue_schur_transform_residual_bound_mono_scalar` specialize the conservative Schur-coordinate residual-bound endpoint by deriving the nonsingular-inverse budget from `NoCommonComplexRightEigenvalue (realMatrixToComplex A) (realMatrixToComplex B)`. The relative endpoints assume a positive reconstructed `Xhat` denominator; the monotone forms allow componentwise enlarged inverse and residual-budget estimator data; the absolute endpoints remove that denominator and now include both exact-budget scalar caps and enlarged-budget monotone/scalar caps. None model rounded Schur/Bartels-Stewart arithmetic or produce a LAPACK-style estimator.
- Latest rectangular determinant practical wrappers: `sylvester_practical_error_bound_of_vecCoeff_det_ne_zero_computed_residual_certificate_rect`, `sylvester_practical_abs_error_bound_of_vecCoeff_det_ne_zero_computed_residual_certificate_rect`, `sylvester_practical_error_bound_of_vecCoeff_det_ne_zero_computed_residual_budget_rect`, and `sylvester_practical_error_bound_of_vecCoeff_det_ne_zero_computed_residual_error_model_rect` lift the determinant/non-floating practical residual surface from square `n n` coefficients to rectangular `m n` Sylvester equations. These are certificate-transfer endpoints and still assume residual-budget or residual-error-model data.
- Latest rectangular determinant practical aliases: `H16_eq16_29_sylvester_practical_error_bound_of_vecCoeff_det_ne_zero_computed_residual_certificate_rect`, `H16_eq16_29_sylvester_practical_abs_error_bound_of_vecCoeff_det_ne_zero_computed_residual_certificate_rect`, `H16_eq16_29_sylvester_practical_error_bound_of_vecCoeff_det_ne_zero_computed_residual_budget_rect`, and `H16_eq16_29_sylvester_practical_error_bound_of_vecCoeff_det_ne_zero_computed_residual_error_model_rect` expose the rectangular determinant/non-floating practical residual endpoints under source-numbered equation (16.29) names. These are aliases over existing certificate-transfer endpoints, not rounded residual arithmetic or estimator production.
- Latest named block no-common-eigenvalue wrappers: the real-Schur adjacent `2 x 2` route now also consumes `NoCommonComplexRightEigenvalue` directly via `sylvesterTwoColumnRealSchurBlockComplexRoot_det_separation_of_disc_no_common_complex_right_eigenvalue` and `sylvesterTwoColumnBlockCoeff_block_and_det_ne_zero_of_twoBlockSpectral_no_common_complex_right_eigenvalue`. These are named-hypothesis adapters over the already proved supplied-global-no-common block route; automatic production of that block/A no-common spectrum certificate remains open.
- Latest direct discriminant producer adapter: the strengthened real-Schur block API can now feed the adjacent-block negative-discriminant side of `sylvesterTwoColumnRealSchurBlock_separation_of_disc_det_separation` and `sylvesterTwoColumnRealQuasiSchurBlockSeparation_of_disc_det_separation`; the shifted determinant separation for `A` remains explicit.
- Latest rotation-scaling block bridge: canonical real `2 x 2` entries `[[alpha,beta],[-beta,alpha]]` with `beta != 0` now prove the negative discriminant needed by the real-Schur block-separation predicate, and package that algebra into the bundled real-quasi-Schur predicate when the usual block-map data and shifted determinant separation are supplied. This is a local adapter for a future stronger real-Schur export; current `real_quasi_schur_blocks` still does not produce those entries.
- Latest real-quasi-Schur bundled separation predicate: `IsSylvesterTwoColumnRealQuasiSchurBlockSeparation` now bundles the current block-map/adjacency data with the explicit real-Schur block separation predicate, and wrappers derive both the adjacent-block/no-block-action pair and adjacent-block/determinant pair. This is an honest adapter layer; it still requires a future stronger real-Schur export to produce the separation predicate automatically.
- Latest bundled-separation solve wrappers: the bundled real-quasi-Schur block-separation predicate now feeds active-block injectivity, surjectivity, bijectivity, unique solve, and nonsingular-inverse solution-identification wrappers. These are downstream consequences of the supplied predicate, not evidence that current `real_quasi_schur_blocks` produces it.
- Latest (16.3) source-numbered alias wave: the existing real supplied left-eigenpair constructive direction, shifted determinant singularity, common-real-eigenvalue obstruction, and determinant-based exclusion corollaries now expose `H16_eq16_3_*` aliases. These aliases deliberately retain the existing real/supplied/one-direction scope and do not claim the full complex Kronecker spectral converse.
- Latest (16.3) symmetric alias addendum: `H16_eq16_3_sylvesterVecCoeff_singular_of_common_eigenvalue`, `H16_eq16_3_no_common_real_eigenpair_of_det_ne_zero`, `H16_eq16_3_no_common_real_eigenpair_of_schurTriangular`, and `H16_eq16_3_no_common_real_left_eigenpair_of_schurTriangular` expose the transpose-eigenpair common-real-eigenvalue obstruction and the supplied Schur-triangular exclusion routes under source-numbered names. These are aliases over existing exact supplied-eigenpair and supplied-factor facts, not the full automatic complex spectral converse or rounded solver analysis.

## Reused from Repository or Mathlib

| Source concept/result | Existing declaration | File/module |
|---|---|---|
| Legacy square matrix product | `matMul` | `LeanFpAnalysis.FP.Analysis.MatrixAlgebra` |
| Rectangular matrix product | `matMulRect`, `rectMatMul` | `LeanFpAnalysis.FP.Analysis.MatrixAlgebra` |
| Frobenius norm and squared norm | `frobNorm`, `frobNormSq`, `frobNorm_matMul_le`, triangle/subtraction lemmas | `LeanFpAnalysis.FP.Analysis.MatrixAlgebra` |
| Orthogonality and norm invariance | `IsOrthogonal`, `frobNormSq_orthogonal_left`, `frobNormSq_orthogonal_right` | `LeanFpAnalysis.FP.Analysis.MatrixAlgebra` |
| Transpose | `matTranspose` | `LeanFpAnalysis.FP.Analysis.MatrixAlgebra` |
| Column-stacking vectorization and Kronecker products | `Matrix.vec`, `Matrix.kronecker`, `Matrix.kronecker_mulVec_vec`, `Matrix.vec_mul_eq_mulVec` | `Mathlib.LinearAlgebra.Matrix.Vec` |
| Finite vector max norm for product-index vectors | Mathlib finite-function norm with `norm_le_pi_norm` and `pi_norm_le_iff_of_nonneg` | imported through existing Mathlib/Matrix infrastructure |

Latest open-row update:
- For the degenerate two-column quasi-triangular block route, `sylvesterTwoColumnBlockCoeff_block_and_det_ne_zero_of_quasiSchur_shifted_det_product_zero` now combines same-block quasi-Schur block-map data with nonsingular shifted column coefficients and the zero coupling-product certificate, yielding both `IsAdjacentQuasiTriangularBlockFn` and determinant nonsingularity for the active two-column coefficient. The underlying direct zero-coupling determinant route now also has active-block solve and nonsingular-inverse block-system wrappers through the `*_of_shifted_det_product_zero` family, and the same zero-coupling route with quasi-Schur provenance is exposed through the `*_of_quasiSchur_shifted_det_product_zero` family. This closes the zero-coupling adapter/solve subcase; the genuinely coupled real-Schur 2x2 route still needs the no-coupled-action/product-shift determinant certificate from structural separation.
- For (16.4)-(16.8), `sylvester_realQuasiSchur_factors` exposes the existing real quasi-Schur decomposition surface directly in the Chapter 16 Sylvester file, and `sylvester_realQuasiSchur_factors_twoBlockSpectral` / `sylvester_realQuasiSchur_transform_solution_iff_twoBlockSpectral` retain the constructed adjacent `2 x 2` spectral certificates in the same Sylvester-facing API. The `sylvesterTriangularShiftedCoeff_*`, `existsUnique_sylvester_triangular_column_step_of_shifted_det`, and `sylvester_triangular_column_step_eq_of_shifted_det` facts package nonsingular shifted triangular column coefficients as exact inverse, injectivity, surjectivity, bijectivity, unique-solve, active column-step, and column-step equality facts. The exact generated-schedule candidate route is now closed under the no-common/two-block spectral hypotheses, and the complex-root separation bridge removes the shifted-determinant premise from the constructed two-block spectral route when the matching `A`-root exclusion is supplied, including the bundled block-separation predicate consumed by traversal adapters. The row remains open only for automatic root-exclusion/determinant/separation production where still supplied by hypotheses and for rounded Schur/Bartels-Stewart residual or estimator integration.
- For the two-column quasi-triangular block route, `sylvesterTwoColumnBlockCoeff_det_ne_zero_of_rightInverse`, `sylvesterTwoColumnBlockCoeff_mulVec_surjective_of_rightInverse`, `sylvesterTwoColumnBlockCoeff_det_ne_zero_of_leftInverse`, and `sylvesterTwoColumnBlockCoeff_mulVec_bijective_of_rightInverse_leftInverse` close determinant/surjectivity/bijectivity consequences of supplied inverse certificates. The determinant route `sylvesterTwoColumnBlockCoeff_nonsingInv_mul`, `sylvesterTwoColumnBlockCoeff_mul_nonsingInv`, `sylvesterTwoColumnBlockCoeff_mulVec_injective_of_det_ne_zero`, `sylvesterTwoColumnBlockCoeff_mulVec_surjective_of_det_ne_zero`, `sylvesterTwoColumnBlockCoeff_mulVec_bijective_of_det_ne_zero`, `sylvesterTwoColumnBlockCoeff_mulVec_eq_zero_iff_of_det_ne_zero`, `existsUnique_sylvesterTwoColumnBlockCoeff_mulVec_of_det_ne_zero`, and `sylvesterTwoColumnBlockSystem_of_nonsingInv_columns` now packages exact nonsingular-inverse, bijectivity, trivial-kernel, and solve facts once `det != 0` is known. `sylvesterTwoColumnBlockSystem_columns_eq_of_det_ne_zero_of_prev_columns_eq` / `sylvesterTwoColumnBlockSystem_activeColumns_eq_of_det_ne_zero_of_prev_columns_eq` use the same determinant certificate for recurrence uniqueness from previous-column agreement. `sylvesterTwoColumnBlockSystem_columns_eq_of_nonsingInv_columns_of_det_ne_zero_of_prev_columns_eq` and its active-vector form combine these ingredients when `X` is supplied by the nonsingular-inverse block formula. `quasiSchur_blockMap_strict_after_adjacent_same_block` and `IsAdjacentQuasiTriangularBlockFn.of_quasiSchur_same_block` now connect exported real quasi-Schur block-map data to the supplied adjacent block predicate for adjacent same-block pairs, and `sylvesterTwoColumnBlockCoeff_block_and_det_ne_zero_of_quasiSchur_no_coupled_block_action` packages that same-block quasi-Schur data plus a supplied no-coupled-action condition into adjacent-block data and determinant nonsingularity. The quasi-Schur/no-coupled determinant bridge now also has direct active-block injectivity, surjectivity, bijectivity, trivial-kernel, unique-solve, and nonsingular-inverse solution-identification wrappers. The missing step is still deriving the no-coupled-action/product-shift determinant certificate from structural separation hypotheses for genuine real-Schur 2x2 blocks.
- For (16.2), entrywise gap assumptions now feed determinant nonsingularity for diagonal and supplied Schur-diagonal Sylvester coefficients and diagonal/supplied spectral Lyapunov coefficients; determinant plus concrete-left-inverse finite-op-norm certificates feed vectorized bijectivity plus unique-solve wrappers for finite, Sylvester, and Lyapunov coefficients; and supplied `SepLowerBound` or positive exact-`sylvesterSepInf` lower bounds now feed concrete Sylvester/Lyapunov vec-coefficient sigma-min, determinant, left/right nonsingular-inverse action, and solution-identification certificates. This closes another source-to-coefficient certificate bridge but not the fully general nondiagonal Kronecker spectral criterion.
- For (16.23)-(16.24), the source `SepLowerBound`, exact-infimum, concrete vec-coefficient sigma-min, finite-op-norm left-inverse, finite-Gram, diagonal, and supplied Schur-diagonal Sylvester condition routes now expose relative first-order wrappers directly. The remaining estimator path is still open because these wrappers specialize residual-budget certificates rather than deriving rounded Lyapunov solves or estimator data.

## Hidden-Hypothesis Summary

- The existing proved square theorems assume explicit Frobenius-norm bounds, `SepLowerBound`, nonzero norm-squared hypotheses where needed, and supplied linearized equations. These are domain/reused-theorem assumptions, not replacements for the target equation.
- `sylvesterSepInf` records the exact infimum object for `sep(A,B)`; `SepLowerBound` is now equivalent to a positive lower bound of that infimum when the feasible ratio set is nonempty, and the feasible set is proved nonempty in positive dimension. The printed minimum form is closed in positive dimension by `exists_sylvesterSep_minimizer`, `isLeast_sylvesterSepRatios`, and `exists_sylvesterSep_ratio_minimizer`.
- `sylvesterBackwardErrorInf` records the backward-error eta quantity as an infimum of nonnegative feasible `IsBackwardError` certificates. The two-sided xi bridge and least-value attainment are proved for this infimum model under the stated positive-weight and nonempty-feasible-set hypotheses, and the SVD optimal-perturbation construction now discharges nonemptiness in `exists_sylvesterBackwardError_minimizer_of_svdOptimalPerturbations`, `sylvesterBackwardErrorInf_mem_sylvesterBackwardErrorValues_of_svdOptimalPerturbations`, and `isLeast_sylvesterBackwardErrorValues_of_svdOptimalPerturbations`.
- `lyapunovBackwardErrorInf` records the Lyapunov-specific eta quantity as an infimum over structured certificates with one tied `DeltaA` perturbation and symmetric `DeltaC`. The two-sided Lyapunov eta/xi bridge and least-value attainment are proved under the stated positive-weight and nonempty-feasible-set hypotheses, with the symmetric-spectral optimizer discharging nonemptiness.
- `LyapunovConditionFirstOrderBound` is an explicit condition-number certificate corresponding to (16.27). A positive `SepLowerBound(A, -A^T)` supplies a safe source-facing Lyapunov condition wrapper via `M = 1/sigma`, with the raw inequality exposed by `lyapunov_first_order_bound_of_sepLowerBound`; a positive lower bound on the exact `sylvesterSepInf A (-A^T)` model supplies both the predicate-level wrapper `lyapunovCond_of_pos_le_sylvesterSepInf_isLyapunovConditionFirstOrderBound`, the raw wrapper `lyapunov_first_order_bound_of_pos_le_sylvesterSepInf`, and the theorem-level wrapper `H16_eq16_27_lyapunov_condition_of_pos_le_sylvesterSepInf`; a positive sigma-min lower bound on the Lyapunov operator supplies the same wrapper via `lyapunovInverseOpBound_of_sigmaMin`, with the raw inequality exposed by `lyapunov_first_order_bound_of_sigmaMin`; a positive lower-bound certificate for the concrete `lyapunovVecCoeff` supplies it via `lyapunovCond_of_vecCoeff_sigmaMin_isLyapunovConditionFirstOrderBound`; a concrete left inverse plus finite operator-2 bound supplies it via `lyapunov_first_order_bound_of_vecCoeff_left_inverse_finiteOpNorm2Le` and `lyapunov_relative_first_order_bound_of_vecCoeff_left_inverse_finiteOpNorm2Le`; a finite Gram eigenvalue lower bound supplies the concrete coefficient/operator lower bound and direct source wrapper via `lyapunovVecCoeff_sigmaMin_of_gram_eigenvalues`, `lyapunovOp_sigmaMin_of_vecCoeff_gram_eigenvalues`, and `H16_eq16_27_lyapunov_condition_of_vecCoeff_gram_eigenvalues`; diagonal entrywise separation supplies such a Gram-eigenvalue lower bound via `lyapunovVecCoeff_diagonal_gram_eigenvalues_ge_of_entrywise_abs_ge`; and supplied orthogonal spectral-diagonal data supplies `sep(A,-A^T)` lower-bound/infimum certificates, operator, coefficient, Gram, and source-shaped relative perturbation bounds via `SepLowerBound_lyapunovSpectralDiagonal_of_entrywise_abs_ge`, `sylvesterSepInf_lyapunovSpectralDiagonal_ge_of_entrywise_abs_ge`, `sylvesterSepInf_lyapunovSpectralDiagonal_ge_of_entrywise_abs_ge_of_pos_dim`, `lyapunovOp_sigmaMin_spectralDiagonal_of_entrywise_abs_ge`, `lyapunovVecCoeff_spectralDiagonal_sigmaMin_of_entrywise_abs_ge`, `lyapunovVecCoeff_spectralDiagonal_gram_eigenvalues_ge_of_entrywise_abs_ge`, `H16_eq16_27_lyapunov_condition_spectralDiagonal_of_vecCoeff_entrywise_abs_ge`, and `H16_eq16_27_lyapunov_condition_spectralDiagonal_of_sep_entrywise_abs_ge`. The remaining exact displayed nondiagonal construction is proving the concrete Gram spectral value or lower bound automatically without assuming supplied spectral factors.
- The Lyapunov perturbation wrappers from `SepLowerBound` and exact-infimum certificates reuse the existing Sylvester perturbation theorem with `B = -A^T` and `DeltaB = -DeltaA^T`, proving the required norm bound for the transposed perturbation explicitly. They keep the nonzero `frobNormSq DeltaX` and nonzero/positive `frobNorm X` assumptions visible because those are premises of the older absolute/relative perturbation theorems.
- `sylvester_schur_transform_identity`, `sylvester_schur_transform_solution_iff`, `sylvesterResidualRect_schur_transform_identity`, `H16_eq16_5_9_sylvesterResidualRect_schur_transform_identity`, `frobNormRect_sylvesterResidualRect_schur_transform`, `H16_eq16_9_frobNormRect_sylvesterResidualRect_schur_transform`, `frobNormRect_sylvesterResidualRect_le_of_schur_transform`, `H16_eq16_9_frobNormRect_sylvesterResidualRect_le_of_schur_transform`, `existsUnique_isSylvesterSolutionRect_schurDiagonal`, `sylvesterVecCoeff_schurDiagonal_det_ne_zero`, `sylvesterOp_sigmaMin_schurDiagonal_of_entrywise_abs_ge`, `sylvesterVecCoeff_schurDiagonal_sigmaMin_of_entrywise_abs_ge`, `sylvesterVecCoeff_schurDiagonal_gram_eigenvalues_ge_of_entrywise_abs_ge`, `SepLowerBound_schurDiagonal_of_entrywise_abs_ge`, `sylvesterSepInf_schurDiagonal_ge_of_entrywise_abs_ge`, `sylvesterSepInf_schurDiagonal_ge_of_entrywise_abs_ge_of_pos_dim`, `existsUnique_isSylvesterSolutionRect_schurTriangular`, and the `sylvesterVecCoeff_schurTriangular_*` vectorized coefficient theorems assume supplied factorizations and orthogonality; the triangular theorems also assume a supplied upper-triangular factor and nonsingular shifted column coefficients. The residual-transport theorems are exact algebraic/norm/bound bridges, not rounded arithmetic models. `sylvester_realQuasiSchur_factors` records real quasi-Schur factor existence, and the current traversal wrappers combine supplied Schur factors with supplied full block determinant certificates, product-shift determinant certificates converted internally, or supplied real-Schur two-block spectral/no-common data to prove exact Schur-coordinate and original-coordinate unique solves. The singleton no-common determinant wrappers additionally discharge shifted singleton determinants from supplied true singleton-fiber data plus global no-common spectrum, the reduced no-common frontier adapters consume those singleton-fiber certificates directly, and the neighbor adapters derive the needed singleton fiber from local predecessor/successor block-label separation. The frontier-boundary helpers and `quasiSchur_exists_frontier_schedule` prove the pure generated schedule, generated-frontier traversal wrappers consume it, and the recursive generated-schedule candidate route supplies exact Schur-coordinate and original-coordinate generated-step witnesses under the no-common/two-block spectral hypotheses. These are not proofs of automatic unsupplied determinant/certificate discovery outside that package, generated Hessenberg-Schur reductions, rounded residual arithmetic, or floating-point stability.
- The two-block spectral root-separation bridge no longer assumes a shifted determinant certificate for the active coupled block; it assumes the source-visible exclusion of the constructed complex block root from `A`. That exclusion is weaker plumbing than the determinant certificate but still must be derived from no-common-spectrum data before claiming a fully automatic structural separation route.
- `SylvesterPsiFirstOrderBound` is an explicit condition-number certificate corresponding to (16.24). The `sqrt 3 * Psi * epsilon` relative perturbation theorem is proved from that certificate, and a positive `SepLowerBound` supplies a safe source-facing `Psi` wrapper via `M = 1/sigma`, with the raw inequality exposed by `sylvester_first_order_bound_of_sepLowerBound`; a positive lower bound on the exact `sylvesterSepInf` model supplies both the predicate-level wrapper `sylvesterPsi_of_pos_le_sylvesterSepInf_isPsiFirstOrderBound`, the raw wrapper `sylvester_first_order_bound_of_pos_le_sylvesterSepInf`, and the theorem-level wrapper `H16_eq16_24_structured_condition_of_pos_le_sylvesterSepInf`; a positive sigma-min lower bound on the Sylvester operator supplies the same wrapper via `sylvesterInverseOpBound_of_sigmaMin`, with the raw inequality exposed by `sylvester_first_order_bound_of_sigmaMin`; a positive lower-bound certificate for the concrete `sylvesterVecCoeff` supplies it via `sylvesterPsi_of_vecCoeff_sigmaMin_isPsiFirstOrderBound`, with raw wrappers for sigma-min and finite Gram-eigenvalue lower bounds; and a concrete left inverse plus `finiteOpNorm2Le` bound supplies it via `sylvesterPsi_of_vecCoeff_left_inverse_finiteOpNorm2Le_isPsiFirstOrderBound`, with the raw inequality exposed by `sylvester_first_order_bound_of_vecCoeff_left_inverse_finiteOpNorm2Le`. **Progress (Split-3B Claude lane, `Analysis/InverseOpNorm2.lean`, import-only):** the spectral core `||P^{-1}||_2 = 1/sigma_min` is proved unconditionally by `rayleigh_lower_bound_of_le_finiteHermitianEigenvalues`, `sigmaMin_mul_vecNorm2_le_matMulVec`, and `vecNorm2_le_inv_sigmaMin_mul_matMulVec`. `Higham16VecNorm.lean` closes the Frobenius/`vec` norm bridge, proves a product-index finite Gram identity and lower-bound bridge, transfers finite Gram eigenvalue lower bounds to the concrete Sylvester and Lyapunov coefficient/operator hypotheses, exposes direct Gram-eigenvalue wrappers for (16.23)-(16.25), (16.27), and (16.28), supplies diagonal plus supplied Schur-diagonal Gram-eigenvalue certificates from coordinate separation, adds a concrete left-inverse route to Sylvester/Lyapunov coefficient sigma-min, Gram, inverse-operator, source-shaped condition, and raw first-order wrappers, and now transfers supplied source `SepLowerBound`/exact-infimum lower-bound certificates into concrete Sylvester/Lyapunov coefficient sigma-min and determinant certificates. The remaining full self-supply gap is constructing/bounding such an inverse certificate automatically for arbitrary nondiagonal coefficients without supplied diagonal factors.
- The general Sylvester concrete-left-inverse and source-sep routes use explicit finite-dimensional certificates rather than proving the full eigenvalue criterion. `SepLowerBound_of_vecCoeff_left_inverse_finiteOpNorm2Le` transfers a supplied left inverse and finite operator-2 bound for `sylvesterVecCoeff n n A B` to `SepLowerBound n A B (1 / M)`, while `sylvesterVecCoeff_sigmaMin_of_sepLowerBound` and `sylvesterVecCoeff_det_ne_zero_of_sepLowerBound` transfer a supplied source `SepLowerBound` back to the concrete coefficient sigma-min/determinant routes. The exact-infimum variants use `SepLowerBound_of_pos_le_sylvesterSepInf` and keep positivity hypotheses visible.
- The current concrete-left-inverse and source-sep Lyapunov routes use explicit finite-dimensional certificates rather than assuming the desired (16.27) condition-number theorem: `lyapunovOp_sigmaMin_of_vecCoeff_left_inverse_finiteOpNorm2Le` transfers the left inverse to an operator sigma-min lower bound, `SepLowerBound_lyapunov_of_vecCoeff_left_inverse_finiteOpNorm2Le` transfers it to a safe `sep(A,-A^T)` certificate, `sylvesterSepInf_lyapunov_ge_of_vecCoeff_left_inverse_finiteOpNorm2Le` exposes the corresponding exact-infimum lower bound in positive dimension, `lyapunov_perturbation_bound_of_vecCoeff_left_inverse_finiteOpNorm2Le` / `lyapunov_relative_perturbation_of_vecCoeff_left_inverse_finiteOpNorm2Le` instantiate the absolute and relative perturbation inequalities, and `lyapunovVecCoeff_mulVec_bijective_of_left_inverse_finiteOpNorm2Le` / `existsUnique_lyapunovVecCoeff_mulVec_of_left_inverse_finiteOpNorm2Le` expose the matching vectorized solve certificates. Conversely, `lyapunovVecCoeff_sigmaMin_of_sepLowerBound` and `lyapunovVecCoeff_det_ne_zero_of_sepLowerBound` transfer supplied `sep(A,-A^T)` lower-bound certificates back into the concrete Lyapunov vec-coefficient routes.
- The current direct sigma-min Lyapunov route also keeps its certificate visible: `SepLowerBound_lyapunov_of_sigmaMin` converts a positive lower bound for the Lyapunov operator into a `sep(A,-A^T)` lower bound, `sylvesterSepInf_lyapunov_ge_of_sigmaMin` transfers it to the exact infimum model in positive dimension, and `lyapunov_perturbation_bound_of_sigmaMin`, `lyapunov_first_order_bound_of_sigmaMin`, and `lyapunov_relative_perturbation_of_sigmaMin` instantiate the same source-shaped first-order inequalities. This does not prove the exact nondiagonal spectral value of the Lyapunov coefficient automatically.
- The explicit solution-witness wrappers strengthen the user-facing certificate surface but keep the same hypotheses visible: determinant, sigma-min, finite-Gram, or concrete-left-inverse data. `existsUnique_finiteMatrix_nonsingInv_mulVec_solution_of_det_ne_zero` and its Sylvester/Lyapunov wrappers prove both the coefficient equation and `x = P^{-1} c` for the unique witness; `existsUnique_isSylvesterSolutionRect_of_sylvesterVecCoeff_det_ne_zero` and `H16_eq16_3_existsUnique_isSylvesterSolutionRect_of_sylvesterVecCoeff_det_ne_zero` turn any Sylvester coefficient determinant certificate into unique solvability of the matrix equation. These do not supply the missing general spectral criterion or construct a coefficient inverse automatically.
- The source-sep/exact-infimum solution-witness wrappers add the same explicit bijectivity, nonsingular-inverse witness, left/right action, and solution-identification surface when the caller supplies `SepLowerBound` or a positive lower bound on `sylvesterSepInf`. They use the proved source-to-coefficient determinant bridge and still keep the separation certificate visible.
- The (16.29) practical-bound theorems assume visible certificates: a left inverse `Pinv * sylvesterVecCoeff = 1`, an entrywise inverse bound `|Pinv| <= PinvAbs`, and an `IsSylvesterComputedResidualBudget` certificate. The residual-budget certificate can be produced from an explicit residual error matrix `dR` with `Rhat = R + dR` and `|dR| <= Ru`; the Schur-coordinate bridges now produce original-coordinate budgets from supplied Schur Frobenius residual-error models, feed those models directly into relative practical endpoints, and use conservative `Rhat = 0` wrappers to produce relative, relative scalar, relative monotone, relative monotone-scalar, denominator-free absolute, and scalar-cap absolute practical endpoints from a supplied Schur residual bound. The floating-point residual model now supplies that certificate for arbitrary `A,B` through `sylvester_practical_error_bound_fl_of_left_inverse` and its scalar/monotone variants when inverse certificates are supplied. Rectangular no-common-complex-spectrum hypotheses now instantiate the same floating residual model directly through `sylvester_practical_error_bound_fl_of_no_common_complex_right_eigenvalue` and its scalar/monotone variants, using the proved determinant/no-common bridge and nonsingular-inverse budget. For square coefficients, `sylvester_practical_error_bound_fl_of_vecCoeff_det_ne_zero`, `sylvester_practical_error_bound_fl_of_vecCoeff_gram_eigenvalues`, `sylvester_practical_error_bound_fl_of_vecCoeff_sigmaMin`, `sylvester_practical_error_bound_fl_of_vecCoeff_left_inverse_finiteOpNorm2Le`, `sylvester_practical_error_bound_fl_of_sepLowerBound`, and `sylvester_practical_error_bound_fl_of_pos_le_sylvesterSepInf` plus their scalar/monotone variants use proved determinant certificates to instantiate the nonsingular inverse and its entrywise absolute-value budget. The non-floating certificate and explicit error-model theorem families similarly have determinant-nonzero square endpoints. The monotone practical wrapper assumes componentwise larger estimated inverse/residual/rounding budgets and proves only the corresponding larger error bound; it is not a proof of a LAPACK estimator. The diagonal, supplied Schur-diagonal, supplied Schur-triangular, separated-diagonal, source-`SepLowerBound`, no-common-complex-spectrum, and exact-infimum floating-point scalar wrappers additionally assume a scalar cap on the already-defined practical budget vector; they do not derive an estimator. The supplied Schur-diagonal and Schur-triangular wrappers discharge the left-inverse and entrywise inverse-bound certificates from proved determinant-nonsingularity theorems for supplied orthogonal factors; the triangular wrappers also assume a supplied upper-triangular factor and shifted diagonal nonsingularity conditions. The strict real-quasi-Schur shifted practical wrappers remove the separate global vec/Kronecker determinant premise by deriving it from a strict `B`-side block map plus supplied shifted triangular column determinant certificates. They still assume supplied Schur-style data and computed-residual certificate/error-model data. They do not prove rounded Schur solve arithmetic, quasi-triangular block handling, or the LAPACK estimator.
- The non-floating practical-bound source wrappers now mirror the floating-point source wrappers for `SepLowerBound`, exact-infimum, determinant, and named no-common-complex-right-eigenvalue certificates across computed-residual certificates, raw budgets, and explicit residual-error models, with scalar/monotone variants where available. The determinant surface now includes rectangular `_rect` endpoints as well as the older square family. They reuse determinant/nonsingular-inverse bridges and do not change the estimator or rounded-solve assumptions.
- The no-common Schur residual-bound endpoints now combine those two certificate routes: `NoCommonComplexRightEigenvalue (realMatrixToComplex A) (realMatrixToComplex B)` supplies the canonical nonsingular-inverse budget, while the supplied Schur-coordinate residual bound supplies the conservative original residual budget through the exact Schur transport with `Rhat = 0`. The family now includes relative, relative scalar, denominator-free absolute, and absolute scalar-cap endpoints; it remains certificate transfer, not rounded solver analysis.
- No new global axioms, `sorry`, `admit`, `unsafe`, or opaque placeholders are introduced by the Chapter 16 companion module.
